Are common voters now expecting free concessions instead of qualitative changes in political governance? Is it now impossible to win elections on the basis of policies to increase private investment, industrial development, free market and limit the role of government? And if a government pursues populist policies, then does the gnawing of educated urban voters against poor governance or political plunder have no political significance?
